SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL

FROM [books] AS [b]

    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Description], [b].[IsRead], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[DateRead]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[DateAdd], CASE
    WHEN [b].[IsRead] = CAST(1 AS bit) THEN [b].[Rate]
    ELSE NULL
END, [b].[Genre], [b].[CoverUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
FROM [books] AS [b]
LEFT JOIN [publishers] AS [p] ON [b].[PublisherId] = [p].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Name], [b0].[Id], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[idbook]
    FROM [book_authors] AS [b0]
    LEFT JOIN [author] AS [a] ON [b0].[idauthor] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [b].[Id] = [t].[idbook]
ORDER BY [b].[Id], [p].[Id], [t].[Id]
